SELECT q3.id, q3.created_at, q3.description, q3.disabled, q3.note_id, q3.title, q3.updated_at, q3.user_id, q3.visibility, q0.id, q0.created_at, q0.display_order, q0.original_question_id, q0.question_snapshot, q0.quiz_id, q0.updated_at, s1.quiz_id, s1.tag_id, s1.id, s1.name, s2.quiz_id, s2.source_id, s2.id, s2.content, s2.created_at, s2.deleted_at, s2.file_path, s2.metadata, s2.raw_html, s2.raw_text, s2.title, s2.type, s2.updated_at, s2.url, s2.user_id
FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility
    FROM quiz AS q
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS q3
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON q3.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s1 ON q3.id = s1.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s2 ON q3.id = s2.quiz_id
ORDER BY q3.id, q0.display_order, q0.id, s1.quiz_id, s1.tag_id, s1.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.source_id

    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s2 ON q3.id = s2.quiz_id
ORDER BY q3.id, q0.display_order, q0.id, s1.quiz_id, s1.tag_id, s1.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.source_id

FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

SELECT s1.id, s1.created_at, s1.description, s1.disabled, s1.note_id, s1.title, s1.updated_at, s1.user_id, s1.visibility, s1.id0, q0.id, q0.created_at, q0.display_order, q0.original_question_id, q0.question_snapshot, q0.quiz_id, q0.updated_at, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s2.name, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id, s3.id, s3.content, s3.created_at, s3.deleted_at, s3.file_path, s3.metadata, s3.raw_html, s3.raw_text, s3.title, s3.type, s3.updated_at, s3.url, s3.user_id, s1.created_at0, s1.email, s1.email_confirmed, s1.email_verification_token, s1.password_hash, s1.password_reset_expiry, s1.password_reset_token, s1.role, s1.status, s1.updated_at0, s1.username
FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

SELECT s1.id, s1.created_at, s1.description, s1.disabled, s1.note_id, s1.title, s1.updated_at, s1.user_id, s1.visibility, s1.id0, q0.id, q0.created_at, q0.display_order, q0.original_question_id, q0.question_snapshot, q0.quiz_id, q0.updated_at, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s2.name, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id, s3.id, s3.content, s3.created_at, s3.deleted_at, s3.file_path, s3.metadata, s3.raw_html, s3.raw_text, s3.title, s3.type, s3.updated_at, s3.url, s3.user_id, s1.created_at0, s1.email, s1.email_confirmed, s1.email_verification_token, s1.password_hash, s1.password_reset_expiry, s1.password_reset_token, s1.role, s1.status, s1.updated_at0, s1.username
FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

SELECT s1.id, s1.created_at, s1.description, s1.disabled, s1.note_id, s1.title, s1.updated_at, s1.user_id, s1.visibility, s1.id0, q0.id, q0.created_at, q0.display_order, q0.original_question_id, q0.question_snapshot, q0.quiz_id, q0.updated_at, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s2.name, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id, s3.id, s3.content, s3.created_at, s3.deleted_at, s3.file_path, s3.metadata, s3.raw_html, s3.raw_text, s3.title, s3.type, s3.updated_at, s3.url, s3.user_id, s1.created_at0, s1.email, s1.email_confirmed, s1.email_verification_token, s1.password_hash, s1.password_reset_expiry, s1.password_reset_token, s1.role, s1.status, s1.updated_at0, s1.username
FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id

FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id

    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id

        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id

SELECT s1.id, s1.created_at, s1.description, s1.disabled, s1.note_id, s1.title, s1.updated_at, s1.user_id, s1.visibility, s1.id0, q0.id, q0.created_at, q0.display_order, q0.original_question_id, q0.question_snapshot, q0.quiz_id, q0.updated_at, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s2.name, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id, s3.id, s3.content, s3.created_at, s3.deleted_at, s3.file_path, s3.metadata, s3.raw_html, s3.raw_text, s3.title, s3.type, s3.updated_at, s3.url, s3.user_id, s1.created_at0, s1.email, s1.email_confirmed, s1.email_verification_token, s1.password_hash, s1.password_reset_expiry, s1.password_reset_token, s1.role, s1.status, s1.updated_at0, s1.username
FROM (
    SELECT q.id, q.created_at, q.description, q.disabled, q.note_id, q.title, q.updated_at, q.user_id, q.visibility, u.id AS id0, u.created_at AS created_at0, u.email, u.email_confirmed, u.email_verification_token, u.password_hash, u.password_reset_expiry, u.password_reset_token, u.role, u.status, u.updated_at AS updated_at0, u.username
    FROM quiz AS q
    INNER JOIN users AS u ON q.user_id = u.id
    WHERE NOT (q.disabled) AND q.id = @id AND NOT (q.disabled)
    LIMIT 1
) AS s1
LEFT JOIN quiz_question AS q0 ON s1.id = q0.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q1.quiz_id, q1.tag_id, t.id, t.name
    FROM quiz_tag AS q1
    INNER JOIN tag AS t ON q1.tag_id = t.id
) AS s2 ON s1.id = s2.quiz_id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT q2.quiz_id, q2.source_id, s0.id, s0.content, s0.created_at, s0.deleted_at, s0.file_path, s0.metadata, s0.raw_html, s0.raw_text, s0.title, s0.type, s0.updated_at, s0.url, s0.user_id
    FROM quiz_source AS q2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT s.id, s.content, s.created_at, s.deleted_at, s.file_path, s.metadata, s.raw_html, s.raw_text, s.title, s.type, s.updated_at, s.url, s.user_id
        FROM source AS s
        WHERE s.deleted_at IS NULL
    ) AS s0 ON q2.source_id = s0.id
) AS s3 ON s1.id = s3.quiz_id
ORDER BY s1.id, s1.id0, q0.display_order, q0.id, s2.quiz_id, s2.tag_id, s2.id, s3.quiz_id, s3.source_id
